[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-buffer-overflow was detected by AddressSanitizer in the Mongoose codebase [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring a fuzzing session. The overflow occurs in the formatted output path, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically within the function `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand its related helper [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_putchar_iobuf_static`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when handling a crafted input. The error manifests as a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone‐byte write just past the end of a stack‐allocated buffer in `mg_vxprintf`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating a memory safety vulnerability.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During a libFuzzer run against the Mongoose HTTP parser, AddressSanitizer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreported a stack-buffer-overflow in the formatting subsystem. The crash trace shows[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma write of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m to an address just beyond the bounds of a local buffer.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a stack-based buffer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmemory corruption[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the printf/fmt code,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich can lead to undefined behavior and potential security issues.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflowing write happens in `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused by [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_putchar_iobuf_static`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, invoked from `scpy` in `fmt.c`.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The immediate overflow target is a stack slot for the temporary buffer [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tmp371`, defined in `mg_vxprintf` at line [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m of `fmt.c`. A write at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceeds the [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m‐byte size of that slot.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The formatting routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mg_vxprintf`, `mg_vsnprintf`, `mg_snprintf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are used[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby `mg_dtoa` in number-to-string conversion and by `mg_log` in logging. The [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow is triggered during HTTP parsing in `mg_http_parse`, as exercised by the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz test harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Affected Code Areas  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To gain a complete understanding of the issue, the following modules should be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreviewed:  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • src/mongoose/src/printf.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mg_pfn_iobuf_private`, `mg_putchar_iobuf_static`, [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Reproduction Context  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
